(function(){

	if(location.hostname.indexOf("news") == -1){

	function showQR(top, imgUrl){
		var QRbox= document.createElement("div");
		var QRboxCSS ={
			'width': "110px",
			'height': "147px",
			'position': "fixed",
			'_position': "absolute",
			'top': top + "px",
			'right': "3px",
			'display':"block",
			'zIndex':100
		};
		for(var key in QRboxCSS){
			QRbox.style[key] = QRboxCSS[key];
		}
	 	if(isIE6){
	 		QRbox.style.position = "absolute";
	 	}

		QRbox.innerHTML="<a href='http://3g.163.com/links/4102' target='_blank'></a>";
		var link =QRbox.getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
		var linkCSS = {
			display:"block",
			width: "100%",
			height: "100%",
			backgroundImage: "url("+imgUrl+")",
			backgroundPosition: "0px 0px"
		};
		for(var key in linkCSS){
			link.style[key] = linkCSS[key]
		}
		document.body.appendChild(QRbox);
		var linkEventMap = {
			"mouseover": function(){
				link.style.backgroundPosition = "-110px 0px";
			},
			"mouseout": function(){
				link.style.backgroundPosition = "0px 0px";
			}
		}
		for(var evt in linkEventMap){
			var func = linkEventMap[evt];
			addEvent(evt, link, func);
		}
		addEvent("scroll", window, function(){
			if(isIE6){
				QRbox.style.top = getScrollTop() + top + "px";
			}
		})
	}
	function addEvent(evt, elem, callback){
		if(elem.addEventListener){
			elem.addEventListener(evt, callback, false)
		} else {
			elem.attachEvent && elem.attachEvent("on"+evt, callback);
		}
	}
	function getScrollTop(){
	    if(typeof pageYOffset!= 'undefined'){
	        //most browsers
	        return pageYOffset;
	    }
	    else{
	        var B= document.body; //IE 'quirks'
	        var D= document.documentElement; //IE with doctype
	        D= (D.clientHeight)? D: B;
	        return D.scrollTop;
	    }
	}
})();

    //日历Start
    function calendar(year, month){
        //Get current Date
        var cDate = new Date();
        var cYear = cDate.getYear();
        if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("MSIE") == -1) {
            cYear = cYear + 1900;
        }
        var cMonth = cDate.getMonth();
        var cDay = cDate.getDate();
        var yearDom = NTES("#setYear");
        var monthDom = NTES("#setMonth");
        if (arguments.length > 1) {
            this.year = year;
            this.month = month - 1;
        }
        else {
            this.year = cYear;
            this.month = cMonth;
            //显示日期
            yearDom.innerHTML = cYear;
            monthDom.innerHTML = cMonth + 1;
        }
        this.date = cDay;
        this.draw(printCalendar);
    }
    //获得星期几
    calendar.prototype.getWeekStr = function(day){
        switch (day) {
            case 0:
                return "星期日";
            case 1:
                return "星期一";
            case 2:
                return "星期二";
            case 3:
                return "星期三";
            case 4:
                return "星期四";
            case 5:
                return "星期五";
            case 6:
                return "星期六";
        }
    }
    //获的月的天数
    calendar.prototype.monthDayNum = function(year, month){
        var tdate = new Date(year, month + 1, 0);
        return tdate.getDate();
    }
    //获的指定1号是星期几
    calendar.prototype.dayInWeek = function(year, month, date){
        var tdate = new Date(year, month, date);
        return tdate.getDay();
    }
    //打印日历
    calendar.prototype.draw = function(callback){
        var year = this.year;
        var month = this.month;
        var currentDay = this.date;
        var firstDayInWeek = this.dayInWeek(year, month, 1);
        var monthDayNum = this.monthDayNum(year, month, 0);
        callback(year, month, currentDay, firstDayInWeek, monthDayNum);
    }
    //上一月 下一月
    function calendarNP(yearID, monthID, state){
        var yearDom = NTES(yearID);
        var monthDom = NTES(monthID);
        var year = parseInt(yearDom.innerHTML);
        var month = parseInt(monthDom.innerHTML);
        if (state == "next") {
            month = month + 1;
            if (month > 12) {
                month = 1;
                year = year + 1;
            }
        }
        if (state == "previous") {
            month = month - 1;
            if (month == 0) {
                month = 12;
                year = year - 1;
            }
        }
        yearDom.innerHTML = year;
        monthDom.innerHTML = month;
        var tcalendar = new calendar(year, month);
    }
    //显示日历
    function printCalendar(year, month, currentDay, firstDayInWeek, monthDayNum){
        var year = year;
        var month = month;
        var currentDay = currentDay;
        var firstDayInWeek = firstDayInWeek;
        var monthDayNum = monthDayNum;
        var displayMonth, displayDay;
        var calendarList = NTES("#calendarList");
        var liarray = [];
        if (month < 10) {
            month = month + 1
            displayMonth = "0" + month;
        }
        else {
            displayMonth = month + 1;
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < firstDayInWeek; i++) {
            liarray.push("<li></li>");
        }
        for (var j = 1; j <= monthDayNum; j++) {
            if (j < 10) {
                displayDay = "0" + j;
            }
            else {
                displayDay = j;
            }
            if (j == currentDay) {
                liarray.push("<li><a class=\"current\" href=\"http://post2.news.163.com/wgethtml/http+!!news.163.com!special!0001386F!index_rank.html!/" + year + "-" + displayMonth + "/" + displayDay + "/12.html\">" + j + "</a></li>");
            }
            else {
                liarray.push("<li><a href=\"http://post2.news.163.com/wgethtml/http+!!news.163.com!special!0001386F!index_rank.html!/" + year + "-" + displayMonth + "/" + displayDay + "/12.html\">" + j + "</a></li>");
            }
        }
        var str = liarray.join("");
        calendarList.innerHTML = str;
    }
    // 显示 隐藏图层
    function PopUpLayer(ctrl, content) {
        var timerId;
        var hide = function() {
            content.style.display = "none";
        };
        this.hide = function(event) {
            timerId = setTimeout(hide, 300);
        };
        ctrl.addEvent("mouseover", function() { content.style.display = "block"; });
        ctrl.addEvent("mouseout", this.hide);
        content.addEvent("mouseout", this.hide);
        content.addEvent("mouseover", function() { clearTimeout(timerId); });
    }
    var calendarLayer = new PopUpLayer(NTES("#getCalendar"), NTES("#calendarBox"));
    $("#preMonth").addEvent(
            "click",
            function(event) {
                calendarNP("#setYear","#setMonth","previous");
                NTES.Event.fix(event).preventDefault();
            }
    );
    $("#nextMonth").addEvent(
            "click",
            function(event) {
                calendarNP("#setYear","#setMonth","next");
                NTES.Event.fix(event).preventDefault();
            }
    );
